function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 151') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.151!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('3p/_overview')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/_overview');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('3p/_overview')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/_overview');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/_overview') != '49a6c5e2ee36160e4d623133b59e89ff42b8e755') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/_overview');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/_overview', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/_overview');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== '49a6c5e2ee36160e4d623133b59e89ff42b8e755') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== 'cc92efdf3e54499f5d56f22a5c15a65986b4cd97') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/_overview');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/_overview');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/_overview')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/_overview', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/_overview') !== '49a6c5e2ee36160e4d623133b59e89ff42b8e755') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/_overview');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'f105cab9a6eb237e7d28593e829138009294e3bf') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'f105cab9a6eb237e7d28593e829138009294e3bf') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '21fb47a68b6ab64f3dae1fa5e269f992c03528f8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'f105cab9a6eb237e7d28593e829138009294e3bf') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.css');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.css') != '8f412bc2fb80f411313d7e013eb024917428e4f2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '8f412bc2fb80f411313d7e013eb024917428e4f2') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== 'f3870106bebf56aaf2c0e483c8bfc899c51a01d0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '8f412bc2fb80f411313d7e013eb024917428e4f2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
		}
	}
}

	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js') !== 'fe0ea404b5011cc2b926de5ad6c7328b83ccd3a3') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js') !== '7f0d81ddd85ad3555e1d9eacad0c9e7a9335a7ac') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js') !== 'fe0ea404b5011cc2b926de5ad6c7328b83ccd3a3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/102_change_email/script.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != 'd42701c9fc21b1734c54d67c6573c65a508ab519') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'd42701c9fc21b1734c54d67c6573c65a508ab519') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'ae41cca086d56919604980ba750b263720689c47') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'd42701c9fc21b1734c54d67c6573c65a508ab519') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}
